 1

 1) India vs Pakistan (group match), 2007 Who would not miss the group match between India and Pakistan in the first T20 World Cup
 agar ise ab tak kaa sabase romaanchak match kaha jaae to galat nahin hoga
 The match was decided by ball out
 donon tiimon ne nirdhaarit overon main 141 ran banaae or match taai ho gaya
 Pakistan needed 12 runs to win the last over and had 4 wickets left
 jabaki aakhri do gendon main 1 ran kii jarurat thi, jabaki misabah wo ek ran nahin bana sake or aakhri gend par ran out ho gaye
 Later, the decision went in favor of India with a ball out
 2)bharat banaam pakistan (final match), 2007isi world cap ke final main bhi donon timen aamane-saamne huin, or har gend par match kaa pasa palata
 Sometimes India bowed in favor of Pakistan
 aakhri over tak vijeta kaa anumaan lagaana mushkil tha
 The breath of the people of both countries was stopped
 joginder sharma ke aakhri over main misbah ke ek galat shot ne match pakistan se chin liya or bharat kii jholii main daal diya
 Pakistan required 13 runs in the last over, and had just one wicket
 pehali do gendon par saat ran banane ke baad misabah ne joginder kii chauthi gend par wicket ke peeche shot maar diya, jise srisanth ne kaich kar liya or pehla vishwa cap team india ke naam hua
 3) Australia vs Zimbabwe, 2007 The World T20 was first played in 2007 and in this very first edition, the Zimbabwean team showed how adept it was to rearrange
 50 overon kaa world cap paanch baar jeet chukiaustralian timis formet main ulatpher kaa shikaar ho gai
 In the 2007 World Cup league match, the team suffered a loss to Zimbabwe
 is nattejey ne har kisi ko jaise sann kar diya
 Australia scored 138 runs while playing first
 zimbabwe kii team ne is lakshya ko sirf ek gend shesh rahete hasil kiya or tii20 world cap kaa sabase bada ulatpher bhi kiya
 4) England vs Netherlands, the first match of the 2009 Second World Cup was very exciting
 kamjor netherland se khelte hue england kaa ye match aakhri gend tak ja pahunchaa
 The Netherlands needed 7 runs in the last over to chase down 162 runs
 is over main broad ne khud kii hi gend par ek kaich choda or phir england ke fielderon ne do ran out ke maukey bhi chode
 The result was that the Netherlands won the match on the last ball of the last over
 5) dakshin africa banaam newjiland, 20092009 world cap ke ek or kareebi match main newjiland ko sirf ek ran se haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 The Kiwi team, chasing just 129 runs, could manage only 127 in 20 overs despite being 5 wickets in hand
 kiwi team ke liye ye haar bhi kabhi naa bhul paane vaali haar rahi
 6) Australia vs Pakistan, the second semi-final match between Australia and Pakistan in the 20102010 World Cup has exceeded every level of thrill
 ek samay lagbhag haar ke kagaar par khadi australia ne is match ko aise jeeta ki kisi ko bharosa hi nahin hua
 At one time, Australia needed 48 runs from 18 balls to win, and only three wickets were in hand
 aise samay main mistar cricket mike hasi ne maatr 24 gendon main 60 ranon kii pari khelkar ek gend shesh rahete hi team ko 192 ranon ke lakshya tak pahunchaa diya
 Australia needed 18 runs to win in the last over
 hasi ne said ajmal ke is over main 22 ran kootakar apni team ko final main pahunchaaya
 7) West Indies vs New Zealand, the match between West Indies and New Zealand reached the Super Over in the 20122012 World Cup group match
 lo scoring hone ke baavjood ye match behad romaanchak rahaa
 The Kiwi team, chasing a target of 140 runs, stayed away from the victory by one run and the match was tied
 baad main match kaa faisla super over se hua, jahaan west indies ne 18 ran chej karke jeet hasil kii
 Till the end, the match kept turning around sometimes
 newjiland ke liye ye haar kabhi naa bhuulane vaali jaisi rahi
 Actress Kunika Lal has filed a case of misconduct against the son of a Mumbai MLA
 kunika laal ne andheri ke vidhayak baldev khosla ke bete siddharth khosla ke khilaaf oshivara thane main cese darj karavaaya he
 Kunika alleges that the mla's son abused her and raped her
 police ne dhara 504 va 506 ke tahat maamla darj kiya he
 On the other hand, MLA Baldev Khosla, while talking to Aaj Tak, categorically denied the case of Badalasuki
 saath hi unhone yah bhi kaha ki agar unke bete se kisi tarah kii galati hui he, to ve maafee maangate hai
 Significantly, Kunika Lal is an actress as well as a member of the Congress party
 baharhaal, police maamle kii chaanbin kar rahi he
 Indian industry said on Saturday that demonetisation will have a short-term impact on the country's economy, so the government should take steps to increase productivity and consumption
 udyog jagat ne aagaamee bajet main company tex ko kam karne par bhi jor diya he
 Representatives of industry boards and exporting organizations said this in a pre-budget discussion with Finance Minister Arun Jaitley on Saturday
 ullekhneey he ki sarkaar ne 500 or 1000 rupee ke noton ko 8 november ko chalan se hataa diya
 Along with this, the government has also been suggested to speed up disinvestment in government companies (psus), reduce corporate tax to 18 percent and decrease MAT
